32:Te3c,## Privacy Policy

*Last updated: 2026-05-25*

CEP Endfield Planner ("we", "our", or "us") is committed to protecting your privacy. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, and share your information when you use our website and services.

### 1. Information We Collect

**Account Information:** When you register an account, we collect your username, email address, and a hashed password. We do not store your plain-text password.

**Usage Data:** We collect data about your interactions with our services, such as the features you use and the time of your visits.

**Planning Data:** We store your weapon selections, essence status, refinement plans, and other planner-related data to enable cloud synchronization between your devices.

**Payment Information:** If you purchase a premium subscription, we collect payment proof submissions. We do not directly process payments — all payment information is handled by third-party payment platforms.

### 2. How We Use Your Information

- To provide and maintain our services
- To synchronize your planning data across devices
- To process your premium subscription
- To communicate with you about your account and updates
- To improve our services based on usage patterns

### 3. Data Storage and Security

We implement appropriate security measures to protect your data. Passwords are hashed using industry-standard algorithms. Your planning data is stored on secure servers and transmitted over encrypted connections.

### 4. Cookies and Tracking

We use essential cookies for authentication and session management. We do not use tracking cookies for advertising or third-party analytics.

### 5. Third-Party Services

We use the following third-party services for specific functions:
- **Cloudflare Turnstile:** For bot protection during login and registration, which collects browser fingerprint data for security verification
- **Cloudflare Workers Observability:** For server-side performance monitoring and telemetry, collecting request latency, error rates, and other operational metrics

### 5a. Analytics Services

We use the following analytics services to understand how our website is used and to improve user experience:
- **Umami Analytics:** Self-hosted web analytics — collects anonymized page views, referrers, and device information
- **Baidu Analytics (百度统计):** Web traffic analysis — collects page views, session data, and visitor behavior
- **Microsoft Clarity:** User behavior analytics — collects heatmaps, session recordings, and interaction data
- **Cloudflare Web Analytics:** Privacy-first analytics via Cloudflare Insights — collects anonymized traffic metrics without cookies

These services may use cookies or similar technologies. You can limit or block these analytics services using browser extensions, ad blockers, or your browser's built-in privacy features.

These services have their own privacy policies governing their use of your data.

### 6. Your Rights

You have the right to:
- Access your personal data
- Correct inaccurate data
- Delete your account and associated data
- Export your planning data
- Withdraw consent for data processing

To exercise these rights, please contact us.

### 7. Children's Privacy

Our services are not directed to children under 13. We do not knowingly collect personal information from children.

### 8. Changes to This Policy

We may update this Privacy Policy from time to time. We will notify you of significant changes by posting a notice on our website.

### 9. Contact Us

If you have questions about this Privacy Policy, please contact us through the channels listed on our website.33:Tc2d,## Terms of Service

CEP Endfield Planner provides planning tools for the game Arknights: Endfield, including essence farming optimization, refinement planning, character guides, and related features.

### 3. User Accounts

- You must provide accurate and complete registration information
